    <section class="description">
     <div class="message-the-recruiter">
      <p>Enviar mensaje directo al anunciante de Adaptive Financial Consulting</p>
      <div class="base-main-card">
       <img class="artdeco-entity-image artdeco-entity-image--profile artdeco-entity-image--circle-4 lazy-load" data-delayed-url="https://media-exp1.licdn.com/dms/image/C4D03AQE5NjBPpQPi9A/profile-displayphoto-shrink_100_100/0/1564397375902?e=1611187200&amp;v=beta&amp;t=DY-UnW_KhJz2WZox4Jm1DqsmAqaYHBi6k7ALlsHVjGA" data-ghost-classes="artdeco-entity-image--ghost artdeco-entity-image--ghost-profile" data-ghost-url="https://static-exp3.licdn.com/sc/h/efkb5179rslll10nmhystl3wx" alt="Eduard Pinilla">
       <div class="base-main-card__info">
        <h3 class="base-main-card__title">Eduard Pinilla</h3>
        <h4 class="base-main-card__subtitle">Talent Acquisition Specialist at Adaptive Financial Consulting</h4>
       </div><a aria-label="Enviar mensaje a Eduard Pinilla" class="message-the-recruiter__cta" href="https://www.linkedin.com/login?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fes%2Elinkedin%2Ecom%2Fin%2Feduard-pinilla-77152911a&amp;emailAddress=&amp;fromSignIn=&amp;trk=public_jobs_message-the-recruiter-cta" data-tracking-control-name="public_jobs_message-the-recruiter-cta" data-tracking-will-navigate>
        <icon class="message-the-recruiter__cta-icon" data-delayed-url="https://static-exp3.licdn.com/sc/h/em62t8ujch4hqqc45owxy6auu" data-tracking-will-navigate /></a>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="description__text description__text--rich">
      <section class="show-more-less-html" data-max-lines="5">
       <div class="show-more-less-html__markup show-more-less-html__markup--clamp-after-5">
        <p><strong>We believe that great software is built by teams where collaboration, mutual respect and a drive for quality are front and centre. We want diverse perspectives, a passion for learning and we want people who care deeply about their work. We simply don't understand how long hours cultures are a source of pride or expected to produce excellence. We don't get how combative, political environments are meant to generate amazing teamwork. We don't want an environment where people dread going to work each day. If you feel the same way, please get in touch for a non-committal chat with a member of our team</strong></p>
        <p><br></p>
        <p><strong>We are Adaptive, where you’ll use the latest technology to design, build and operate bespoke, real-time, front-to-back solutions for tier-one investment banks and commodity trading firms financial clients using the latest technology, in flat teams where innovation and collaboration are the backbones of our success.</strong></p>
        <p><br></p>
        <p>As a Java Developer, you will</p>
        <ul>
         <li>participate in the team effort to build and release quality financial software in a timely manner.</li>
         <li>You will be involved in the technical design and implementation of a distributed, multi-region, multi-platform architecture.</li>
         <li>You will be working work in a test-driven, Agile development environment.</li>
        </ul>
        <p><br></p>
        <p><strong>Required skills and experience:</strong></p>
        <ul>
         <li>Solid, professional experience of server-side software development experience preferably in (but not restricted to) Java</li>
         <li>Knowledge of scripting language (e.g. Python)</li>
         <li>Passionate about building distributed, scalable, reliable, and performant software</li>
         <li>Experience with financial systems is a plus</li>
         <li>Deep knowledge of concurrency, resiliency, caching, HTTP and REST</li>
         <li>Even-tempered and able to remain focused on solving production issues when they arise</li>
         <li>Experience working in an Agile environment (Scrum, Kanban)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</li>
         <li>BSc/MSc in Computer Science or equivalent</li>
         <li>Excellent communication skills</li>
         <li>Good English language skills are great to have (but we do offer classes)</li>
         <li>Experience working with distributed teams</li>
        </ul>
        <p><br></p>
        <p><strong>Personal qualities:</strong></p>
        <ul>
         <li>Strong desire to raise the bar for your team technically</li>
         <li>Tenacious, curious, and collaborative in all aspects of your work</li>
         <li>A quick learner with excellent communication skills</li>
        </ul>
        <p><br></p>
        <p><strong>About us:</strong></p>
        <ul>
         <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Competitive Salary</li>
         <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Great benefits package</li>
         <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;No politics</li>
         <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;No cumbersome hierarchy: our teams feel free to speak up, to make suggestions and raise concerns</li>
         <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Collaborative team environment: we all work together, respect each other and pitch in</li>
         <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Smart, welcoming and motivated colleagues</li>
         <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Good work/life balance</li>
        </ul>
        <p><br></p>
        <p><strong>Some of our success stories include:</strong></p>
        <p><br></p>
        <p><em>An app store that allows users to browse available apps and install to their desktop without Administrator rights. The system provides an auto-update mechanism and also captures usage statistics</em></p>
        <p><br></p>
        <p><em>Adaptive brought our experience in large scale e-commerce platforms to quickly specify and&nbsp;agree&nbsp;an architecture with the client. The design enabled rapid development in the short term but also granted flexibility and agility in the long term.</em></p>
        <p><br></p>
        <p><strong>The Small Print</strong></p>
        <p>Please note that the successful candidate will need to have a background check.</p>
        <p>Adaptive's Privacy Notice for Candidates - https://weareadaptive.com/privacy-notice-applicants-adaptive-financial-consulting-ltd/</p>

    <section class="description">
     <div class="message-the-recruiter">
      <p>Enviar mensaje directo al anunciante de Adaptive Financial Consulting</p>
      <div class="base-main-card">
       <img class="artdeco-entity-image artdeco-entity-image--profile artdeco-entity-image--circle-4 lazy-load" data-delayed-url="https://media-exp1.licdn.com/dms/image/C4D03AQE5NjBPpQPi9A/profile-displayphoto-shrink_100_100/0/1564397375902?e=1611187200&amp;v=beta&amp;t=DY-UnW_KhJz2WZox4Jm1DqsmAqaYHBi6k7ALlsHVjGA" data-ghost-classes="artdeco-entity-image--ghost artdeco-entity-image--ghost-profile" data-ghost-url="https://static-exp3.licdn.com/sc/h/efkb5179rslll10nmhystl3wx" alt="Eduard Pinilla">
       <div class="base-main-card__info">
        <h3 class="base-main-card__title">Eduard Pinilla</h3>
        <h4 class="base-main-card__subtitle">Talent Acquisition Specialist at Adaptive Financial Consulting</h4>
       </div><a aria-label="Enviar mensaje a Eduard Pinilla" class="message-the-recruiter__cta" href="https://www.linkedin.com/login?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fes%2Elinkedin%2Ecom%2Fin%2Feduard-pinilla-77152911a&amp;emailAddress=&amp;fromSignIn=&amp;trk=public_jobs_message-the-recruiter-cta" data-tracking-control-name="public_jobs_message-the-recruiter-cta" data-tracking-will-navigate>
        <icon class="message-the-recruiter__cta-icon" data-delayed-url="https://static-exp3.licdn.com/sc/h/em62t8ujch4hqqc45owxy6auu" data-tracking-will-navigate /></a>
      </div>
     </div>
     <div class="description__text description__text--rich">
      <section class="show-more-less-html" data-max-lines="5">
       <div class="show-more-less-html__markup show-more-less-html__markup--clamp-after-5">
        <p><strong>We believe that great software is built by teams where collaboration, mutual respect and a drive for quality are front and centre. We want diverse perspectives, a passion for learning and we want people who care deeply about their work. We simply don't understand how long hours cultures are a source of pride or expected to produce excellence. We don't get how combative, political environments are meant to generate amazing teamwork. We don't want an environment where people dread going to work each day. If you feel the same way, please get in touch for a non-committal chat with a member of our team</strong></p>
        <p><br></p>
        <p><strong>We are Adaptive, where you’ll use the latest technology to design, build and operate bespoke, real-time, front-to-back solutions for tier-one investment banks and commodity trading firms financial clients using the latest technology, in flat teams where innovation and collaboration are the backbones of our success.</strong></p>
        <p><br></p>
        <p>As a Java Developer, you will</p>
        <ul>
         <li>participate in the team effort to build and release quality financial software in a timely manner.</li>
         <li>You will be involved in the technical design and implementation of a distributed, multi-region, multi-platform architecture.</li>
         <li>You will be working work in a test-driven, Agile development environment.</li>
        </ul>
        <p><br></p>
        <p><strong>Required skills and experience:</strong></p>
        <ul>
         <li>Solid, professional experience of server-side software development experience preferably in (but not restricted to) Java</li>
         <li>Knowledge of scripting language (e.g. Python)</li>
         <li>Passionate about building distributed, scalable, reliable, and performant software</li>
         <li>Experience with financial systems is a plus</li>
         <li>Deep knowledge of concurrency, resiliency, caching, HTTP and REST</li>
         <li>Even-tempered and able to remain focused on solving production issues when they arise</li>
         <li>Experience working in an Agile environment (Scrum, Kanban)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</li>
         <li>BSc/MSc in Computer Science or equivalent</li>
         <li>Excellent communication skills</li>
         <li>Good English language skills are great to have (but we do offer classes)</li>
         <li>Experience working with distributed teams</li>
        </ul>
        <p><br></p>
        <p><strong>Personal qualities:</strong></p>
        <ul>
         <li>Strong desire to raise the bar for your team technically</li>
         <li>Tenacious, curious, and collaborative in all aspects of your work</li>
         <li>A quick learner with excellent communication skills</li>
        </ul>
        <p><br></p>
        <p><strong>About us:</strong></p>
        <ul>
         <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Competitive Salary</li>
         <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Great benefits package</li>
         <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;No politics</li>
         <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;No cumbersome hierarchy: our teams feel free to speak up, to make suggestions and raise concerns</li>
         <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Collaborative team environment: we all work together, respect each other and pitch in</li>
         <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Smart, welcoming and motivated colleagues</li>
         <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Good work/life balance</li>
        </ul>
        <p><br></p>
        <p><strong>Some of our success stories include:</strong></p>
        <p><br></p>
        <p><em>An app store that allows users to browse available apps and install to their desktop without Administrator rights. The system provides an auto-update mechanism and also captures usage statistics</em></p>
        <p><br></p>
        <p><em>Adaptive brought our experience in large scale e-commerce platforms to quickly specify and&nbsp;agree&nbsp;an architecture with the client. The design enabled rapid development in the short term but also granted flexibility and agility in the long term.</em></p>
        <p><br></p>
        <p><strong>The Small Print</strong></p>
        <p>Please note that the successful candidate will need to have a background check.</p>
        <p>Adaptive's Privacy Notice for Candidates - https://weareadaptive.com/privacy-notice-applicants-adaptive-financial-consulting-ltd/</p>

        <icon class="show-more-less-html__button-icon" data-delayed-url="https://static-exp3.licdn.com/sc/h/cyolgscd0imw2ldqppkrb84vo" /></button><button class="show-more-less-html__button show-more-less-html__button--less" data-tracking-control-name="public_jobs_show-less-html-btn" aria-label="Mostrar menos" aria-expanded="true">Mostrar menos

   <section class="description">
    <div class="message-the-recruiter">
     <p>Enviar mensaje directo al anunciante de Adaptive Financial Consulting</p>
     <div class="base-main-card">
      <img class="artdeco-entity-image artdeco-entity-image--profile artdeco-entity-image--circle-4 lazy-load" data-delayed-url="https://media-exp1.licdn.com/dms/image/C4D03AQE5NjBPpQPi9A/profile-displayphoto-shrink_100_100/0/1564397375902?e=1611187200&amp;v=beta&amp;t=DY-UnW_KhJz2WZox4Jm1DqsmAqaYHBi6k7ALlsHVjGA" data-ghost-classes="artdeco-entity-image--ghost artdeco-entity-image--ghost-profile" data-ghost-url="https://static-exp3.licdn.com/sc/h/efkb5179rslll10nmhystl3wx" alt="Eduard Pinilla">
      <div class="base-main-card__info">
       <h3 class="base-main-card__title">Eduard Pinilla</h3>
       <h4 class="base-main-card__subtitle">Talent Acquisition Specialist at Adaptive Financial Consulting</h4>
      </div><a aria-label="Enviar mensaje a Eduard Pinilla" class="message-the-recruiter__cta" href="https://www.linkedin.com/login?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fes%2Elinkedin%2Ecom%2Fin%2Feduard-pinilla-77152911a&amp;emailAddress=&amp;fromSignIn=&amp;trk=public_jobs_message-the-recruiter-cta" data-tracking-control-name="public_jobs_message-the-recruiter-cta" data-tracking-will-navigate>
       <icon class="message-the-recruiter__cta-icon" data-delayed-url="https://static-exp3.licdn.com/sc/h/em62t8ujch4hqqc45owxy6auu" data-tracking-will-navigate /></a>
     </div>
    </div>
    <div class="description__text description__text--rich">
     <section class="show-more-less-html" data-max-lines="5">
      <div class="show-more-less-html__markup show-more-less-html__markup--clamp-after-5">
       <p><strong>We believe that great software is built by teams where collaboration, mutual respect and a drive for quality are front and centre. We want diverse perspectives, a passion for learning and we want people who care deeply about their work. We simply don't understand how long hours cultures are a source of pride or expected to produce excellence. We don't get how combative, political environments are meant to generate amazing teamwork. We don't want an environment where people dread going to work each day. If you feel the same way, please get in touch for a non-committal chat with a member of our team</strong></p>
       <p><br></p>
       <p><strong>We are Adaptive, where you’ll use the latest technology to design, build and operate bespoke, real-time, front-to-back solutions for tier-one investment banks and commodity trading firms financial clients using the latest technology, in flat teams where innovation and collaboration are the backbones of our success.</strong></p>
       <p><br></p>
       <p>As a Java Developer, you will</p>
       <ul>
        <li>participate in the team effort to build and release quality financial software in a timely manner.</li>
        <li>You will be involved in the technical design and implementation of a distributed, multi-region, multi-platform architecture.</li>
        <li>You will be working work in a test-driven, Agile development environment.</li>
       </ul>
       <p><br></p>
       <p><strong>Required skills and experience:</strong></p>
       <ul>
        <li>Solid, professional experience of server-side software development experience preferably in (but not restricted to) Java</li>
        <li>Knowledge of scripting language (e.g. Python)</li>
        <li>Passionate about building distributed, scalable, reliable, and performant software</li>
        <li>Experience with financial systems is a plus</li>
        <li>Deep knowledge of concurrency, resiliency, caching, HTTP and REST</li>
        <li>Even-tempered and able to remain focused on solving production issues when they arise</li>
        <li>Experience working in an Agile environment (Scrum, Kanban)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</li>
        <li>BSc/MSc in Computer Science or equivalent</li>
        <li>Excellent communication skills</li>
        <li>Good English language skills are great to have (but we do offer classes)</li>
        <li>Experience working with distributed teams</li>
       </ul>
       <p><br></p>
       <p><strong>Personal qualities:</strong></p>
       <ul>
        <li>Strong desire to raise the bar for your team technically</li>
        <li>Tenacious, curious, and collaborative in all aspects of your work</li>
        <li>A quick learner with excellent communication skills</li>
       </ul>
       <p><br></p>
       <p><strong>About us:</strong></p>
       <ul>
        <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Competitive Salary</li>
        <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Great benefits package</li>
        <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;No politics</li>
        <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;No cumbersome hierarchy: our teams feel free to speak up, to make suggestions and raise concerns</li>
        <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Collaborative team environment: we all work together, respect each other and pitch in</li>
        <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Smart, welcoming and motivated colleagues</li>
        <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Good work/life balance</li>
       </ul>
       <p><br></p>
       <p><strong>Some of our success stories include:</strong></p>
       <p><br></p>
       <p><em>An app store that allows users to browse available apps and install to their desktop without Administrator rights. The system provides an auto-update mechanism and also captures usage statistics</em></p>
       <p><br></p>
       <p><em>Adaptive brought our experience in large scale e-commerce platforms to quickly specify and&nbsp;agree&nbsp;an architecture with the client. The design enabled rapid development in the short term but also granted flexibility and agility in the long term.</em></p>
       <p><br></p>
       <p><strong>The Small Print</strong></p>
       <p>Please note that the successful candidate will need to have a background check.</p>
       <p>Adaptive's Privacy Notice for Candidates - https://weareadaptive.com/privacy-notice-applicants-adaptive-financial-consulting-ltd/</p>

  <section class="description">
   <div class="message-the-recruiter">
    <p>Enviar mensaje directo al anunciante de Adaptive Financial Consulting</p>
    <div class="base-main-card">
     <img class="artdeco-entity-image artdeco-entity-image--profile artdeco-entity-image--circle-4 lazy-load" data-delayed-url="https://media-exp1.licdn.com/dms/image/C4D03AQE5NjBPpQPi9A/profile-displayphoto-shrink_100_100/0/1564397375902?e=1611187200&amp;v=beta&amp;t=DY-UnW_KhJz2WZox4Jm1DqsmAqaYHBi6k7ALlsHVjGA" data-ghost-classes="artdeco-entity-image--ghost artdeco-entity-image--ghost-profile" data-ghost-url="https://static-exp3.licdn.com/sc/h/efkb5179rslll10nmhystl3wx" alt="Eduard Pinilla">
     <div class="base-main-card__info">
      <h3 class="base-main-card__title">Eduard Pinilla</h3>
      <h4 class="base-main-card__subtitle">Talent Acquisition Specialist at Adaptive Financial Consulting</h4>
     </div><a aria-label="Enviar mensaje a Eduard Pinilla" class="message-the-recruiter__cta" href="https://www.linkedin.com/login?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fes%2Elinkedin%2Ecom%2Fin%2Feduard-pinilla-77152911a&amp;emailAddress=&amp;fromSignIn=&amp;trk=public_jobs_message-the-recruiter-cta" data-tracking-control-name="public_jobs_message-the-recruiter-cta" data-tracking-will-navigate>
      <icon class="message-the-recruiter__cta-icon" data-delayed-url="https://static-exp3.licdn.com/sc/h/em62t8ujch4hqqc45owxy6auu" data-tracking-will-navigate /></a>
    </div>
   </div>
   <div class="description__text description__text--rich">
    <section class="show-more-less-html" data-max-lines="5">
     <div class="show-more-less-html__markup show-more-less-html__markup--clamp-after-5">
      <p><strong>We believe that great software is built by teams where collaboration, mutual respect and a drive for quality are front and centre. We want diverse perspectives, a passion for learning and we want people who care deeply about their work. We simply don't understand how long hours cultures are a source of pride or expected to produce excellence. We don't get how combative, political environments are meant to generate amazing teamwork. We don't want an environment where people dread going to work each day. If you feel the same way, please get in touch for a non-committal chat with a member of our team</strong></p>
      <p><br></p>
      <p><strong>We are Adaptive, where you’ll use the latest technology to design, build and operate bespoke, real-time, front-to-back solutions for tier-one investment banks and commodity trading firms financial clients using the latest technology, in flat teams where innovation and collaboration are the backbones of our success.</strong></p>
      <p><br></p>
      <p>As a Java Developer, you will</p>
      <ul>
       <li>participate in the team effort to build and release quality financial software in a timely manner.</li>
       <li>You will be involved in the technical design and implementation of a distributed, multi-region, multi-platform architecture.</li>
       <li>You will be working work in a test-driven, Agile development environment.</li>
      </ul>
      <p><br></p>
      <p><strong>Required skills and experience:</strong></p>
      <ul>
       <li>Solid, professional experience of server-side software development experience preferably in (but not restricted to) Java</li>
       <li>Knowledge of scripting language (e.g. Python)</li>
       <li>Passionate about building distributed, scalable, reliable, and performant software</li>
       <li>Experience with financial systems is a plus</li>
       <li>Deep knowledge of concurrency, resiliency, caching, HTTP and REST</li>
       <li>Even-tempered and able to remain focused on solving production issues when they arise</li>
       <li>Experience working in an Agile environment (Scrum, Kanban)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</li>
       <li>BSc/MSc in Computer Science or equivalent</li>
       <li>Excellent communication skills</li>
       <li>Good English language skills are great to have (but we do offer classes)</li>
       <li>Experience working with distributed teams</li>
      </ul>
      <p><br></p>
      <p><strong>Personal qualities:</strong></p>
      <ul>
       <li>Strong desire to raise the bar for your team technically</li>
       <li>Tenacious, curious, and collaborative in all aspects of your work</li>
       <li>A quick learner with excellent communication skills</li>
      </ul>
      <p><br></p>
      <p><strong>About us:</strong></p>
      <ul>
       <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Competitive Salary</li>
       <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Great benefits package</li>
       <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;No politics</li>
       <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;No cumbersome hierarchy: our teams feel free to speak up, to make suggestions and raise concerns</li>
       <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Collaborative team environment: we all work together, respect each other and pitch in</li>
       <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Smart, welcoming and motivated colleagues</li>
       <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Good work/life balance</li>
      </ul>
      <p><br></p>
      <p><strong>Some of our success stories include:</strong></p>
      <p><br></p>
      <p><em>An app store that allows users to browse available apps and install to their desktop without Administrator rights. The system provides an auto-update mechanism and also captures usage statistics</em></p>
      <p><br></p>
      <p><em>Adaptive brought our experience in large scale e-commerce platforms to quickly specify and&nbsp;agree&nbsp;an architecture with the client. The design enabled rapid development in the short term but also granted flexibility and agility in the long term.</em></p>
      <p><br></p>
      <p><strong>The Small Print</strong></p>
      <p>Please note that the successful candidate will need to have a background check.</p>
      <p>Adaptive's Privacy Notice for Candidates - https://weareadaptive.com/privacy-notice-applicants-adaptive-financial-consulting-ltd/</p>

 <section class="description">
  <div class="message-the-recruiter">
   <p>Enviar mensaje directo al anunciante de Adaptive Financial Consulting</p>
   <div class="base-main-card">
    <img class="artdeco-entity-image artdeco-entity-image--profile artdeco-entity-image--circle-4 lazy-load" data-delayed-url="https://media-exp1.licdn.com/dms/image/C4D03AQE5NjBPpQPi9A/profile-displayphoto-shrink_100_100/0/1564397375902?e=1611187200&amp;v=beta&amp;t=DY-UnW_KhJz2WZox4Jm1DqsmAqaYHBi6k7ALlsHVjGA" data-ghost-classes="artdeco-entity-image--ghost artdeco-entity-image--ghost-profile" data-ghost-url="https://static-exp3.licdn.com/sc/h/efkb5179rslll10nmhystl3wx" alt="Eduard Pinilla">
    <div class="base-main-card__info">
     <h3 class="base-main-card__title">Eduard Pinilla</h3>
     <h4 class="base-main-card__subtitle">Talent Acquisition Specialist at Adaptive Financial Consulting</h4>
    </div><a aria-label="Enviar mensaje a Eduard Pinilla" class="message-the-recruiter__cta" href="https://www.linkedin.com/login?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fes%2Elinkedin%2Ecom%2Fin%2Feduard-pinilla-77152911a&amp;emailAddress=&amp;fromSignIn=&amp;trk=public_jobs_message-the-recruiter-cta" data-tracking-control-name="public_jobs_message-the-recruiter-cta" data-tracking-will-navigate>
     <icon class="message-the-recruiter__cta-icon" data-delayed-url="https://static-exp3.licdn.com/sc/h/em62t8ujch4hqqc45owxy6auu" data-tracking-will-navigate /></a>
   </div>
  </div>
  <div class="description__text description__text--rich">
   <section class="show-more-less-html" data-max-lines="5">
    <div class="show-more-less-html__markup show-more-less-html__markup--clamp-after-5">
     <p><strong>We believe that great software is built by teams where collaboration, mutual respect and a drive for quality are front and centre. We want diverse perspectives, a passion for learning and we want people who care deeply about their work. We simply don't understand how long hours cultures are a source of pride or expected to produce excellence. We don't get how combative, political environments are meant to generate amazing teamwork. We don't want an environment where people dread going to work each day. If you feel the same way, please get in touch for a non-committal chat with a member of our team</strong></p>
     <p><br></p>
     <p><strong>We are Adaptive, where you’ll use the latest technology to design, build and operate bespoke, real-time, front-to-back solutions for tier-one investment banks and commodity trading firms financial clients using the latest technology, in flat teams where innovation and collaboration are the backbones of our success.</strong></p>
     <p><br></p>
     <p>As a Java Developer, you will</p>
     <ul>
      <li>participate in the team effort to build and release quality financial software in a timely manner.</li>
      <li>You will be involved in the technical design and implementation of a distributed, multi-region, multi-platform architecture.</li>
      <li>You will be working work in a test-driven, Agile development environment.</li>
     </ul>
     <p><br></p>
     <p><strong>Required skills and experience:</strong></p>
     <ul>
      <li>Solid, professional experience of server-side software development experience preferably in (but not restricted to) Java</li>
      <li>Knowledge of scripting language (e.g. Python)</li>
      <li>Passionate about building distributed, scalable, reliable, and performant software</li>
      <li>Experience with financial systems is a plus</li>
      <li>Deep knowledge of concurrency, resiliency, caching, HTTP and REST</li>
      <li>Even-tempered and able to remain focused on solving production issues when they arise</li>
      <li>Experience working in an Agile environment (Scrum, Kanban)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</li>
      <li>BSc/MSc in Computer Science or equivalent</li>
      <li>Excellent communication skills</li>
      <li>Good English language skills are great to have (but we do offer classes)</li>
      <li>Experience working with distributed teams</li>
     </ul>
     <p><br></p>
     <p><strong>Personal qualities:</strong></p>
     <ul>
      <li>Strong desire to raise the bar for your team technically</li>
      <li>Tenacious, curious, and collaborative in all aspects of your work</li>
      <li>A quick learner with excellent communication skills</li>
     </ul>
     <p><br></p>
     <p><strong>About us:</strong></p>
     <ul>
      <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Competitive Salary</li>
      <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Great benefits package</li>
      <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;No politics</li>
      <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;No cumbersome hierarchy: our teams feel free to speak up, to make suggestions and raise concerns</li>
      <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Collaborative team environment: we all work together, respect each other and pitch in</li>
      <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Smart, welcoming and motivated colleagues</li>
      <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Good work/life balance</li>
     </ul>
     <p><br></p>
     <p><strong>Some of our success stories include:</strong></p>
     <p><br></p>
     <p><em>An app store that allows users to browse available apps and install to their desktop without Administrator rights. The system provides an auto-update mechanism and also captures usage statistics</em></p>
     <p><br></p>
     <p><em>Adaptive brought our experience in large scale e-commerce platforms to quickly specify and&nbsp;agree&nbsp;an architecture with the client. The design enabled rapid development in the short term but also granted flexibility and agility in the long term.</em></p>
     <p><br></p>
     <p><strong>The Small Print</strong></p>
     <p>Please note that the successful candidate will need to have a background check.</p>
     <p>Adaptive's Privacy Notice for Candidates - https://weareadaptive.com/privacy-notice-applicants-adaptive-financial-consulting-ltd/</p>

   <div class="base-main-card__info">
    <h3 class="base-main-card__title">Eduard Pinilla</h3>
    <h4 class="base-main-card__subtitle">Talent Acquisition Specialist at Adaptive Financial Consulting</h4>
   </div><a aria-label="Enviar mensaje a Eduard Pinilla" class="message-the-recruiter__cta" href="https://www.linkedin.com/login?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fes%2Elinkedin%2Ecom%2Fin%2Feduard-pinilla-77152911a&amp;emailAddress=&amp;fromSignIn=&amp;trk=public_jobs_message-the-recruiter-cta" data-tracking-control-name="public_jobs_message-the-recruiter-cta" data-tracking-will-navigate>

 <div class="description__text description__text--rich">
  <section class="show-more-less-html" data-max-lines="5">
   <div class="show-more-less-html__markup show-more-less-html__markup--clamp-after-5">
    <p><strong>We believe that great software is built by teams where collaboration, mutual respect and a drive for quality are front and centre. We want diverse perspectives, a passion for learning and we want people who care deeply about their work. We simply don't understand how long hours cultures are a source of pride or expected to produce excellence. We don't get how combative, political environments are meant to generate amazing teamwork. We don't want an environment where people dread going to work each day. If you feel the same way, please get in touch for a non-committal chat with a member of our team</strong></p>
    <p><br></p>
    <p><strong>We are Adaptive, where you’ll use the latest technology to design, build and operate bespoke, real-time, front-to-back solutions for tier-one investment banks and commodity trading firms financial clients using the latest technology, in flat teams where innovation and collaboration are the backbones of our success.</strong></p>
    <p><br></p>
    <p>As a Java Developer, you will</p>
    <ul>
     <li>participate in the team effort to build and release quality financial software in a timely manner.</li>
     <li>You will be involved in the technical design and implementation of a distributed, multi-region, multi-platform architecture.</li>
     <li>You will be working work in a test-driven, Agile development environment.</li>
    </ul>
    <p><br></p>
    <p><strong>Required skills and experience:</strong></p>
    <ul>
     <li>Solid, professional experience of server-side software development experience preferably in (but not restricted to) Java</li>
     <li>Knowledge of scripting language (e.g. Python)</li>
     <li>Passionate about building distributed, scalable, reliable, and performant software</li>
     <li>Experience with financial systems is a plus</li>
     <li>Deep knowledge of concurrency, resiliency, caching, HTTP and REST</li>
     <li>Even-tempered and able to remain focused on solving production issues when they arise</li>
     <li>Experience working in an Agile environment (Scrum, Kanban)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</li>
     <li>BSc/MSc in Computer Science or equivalent</li>
     <li>Excellent communication skills</li>
     <li>Good English language skills are great to have (but we do offer classes)</li>
     <li>Experience working with distributed teams</li>
    </ul>
    <p><br></p>
    <p><strong>Personal qualities:</strong></p>
    <ul>
     <li>Strong desire to raise the bar for your team technically</li>
     <li>Tenacious, curious, and collaborative in all aspects of your work</li>
     <li>A quick learner with excellent communication skills</li>
    </ul>
    <p><br></p>
    <p><strong>About us:</strong></p>
    <ul>
     <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Competitive Salary</li>
     <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Great benefits package</li>
     <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;No politics</li>
     <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;No cumbersome hierarchy: our teams feel free to speak up, to make suggestions and raise concerns</li>
     <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Collaborative team environment: we all work together, respect each other and pitch in</li>
     <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Smart, welcoming and motivated colleagues</li>
     <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Good work/life balance</li>
    </ul>
    <p><br></p>
    <p><strong>Some of our success stories include:</strong></p>
    <p><br></p>
    <p><em>An app store that allows users to browse available apps and install to their desktop without Administrator rights. The system provides an auto-update mechanism and also captures usage statistics</em></p>
    <p><br></p>
    <p><em>Adaptive brought our experience in large scale e-commerce platforms to quickly specify and&nbsp;agree&nbsp;an architecture with the client. The design enabled rapid development in the short term but also granted flexibility and agility in the long term.</em></p>
    <p><br></p>
    <p><strong>The Small Print</strong></p>
    <p>Please note that the successful candidate will need to have a background check.</p>
    <p>Adaptive's Privacy Notice for Candidates - https://weareadaptive.com/privacy-notice-applicants-adaptive-financial-consulting-ltd/</p>

 <h4 class="base-main-card__subtitle">Talent Acquisition Specialist at Adaptive Financial Consulting</h4>
</div>
<h3 class="base-main-card__title">Eduard Pinilla</h3>
<h4 class="base-main-card__subtitle">Talent Acquisition Specialist at Adaptive Financial Consulting</h4>
<a aria-label="Enviar mensaje a Eduard Pinilla" class="message-the-recruiter__cta" href="https://www.linkedin.com/login?session_redirect=https%3A%2F%2Fes%2Elinkedin%2Ecom%2Fin%2Feduard-pinilla-77152911a&amp;emailAddress=&amp;fromSignIn=&amp;trk=public_jobs_message-the-recruiter-cta" data-tracking-control-name="public_jobs_message-the-recruiter-cta" data-tracking-will-navigate>
 <icon class="message-the-recruiter__cta-icon" data-delayed-url="https://static-exp3.licdn.com/sc/h/em62t8ujch4hqqc45owxy6auu" data-tracking-will-navigate /></a>
<icon class="message-the-recruiter__cta-icon" data-delayed-url="https://static-exp3.licdn.com/sc/h/em62t8ujch4hqqc45owxy6auu" data-tracking-will-navigate />
<div class="description__text description__text--rich">
 <section class="show-more-less-html" data-max-lines="5">
  <div class="show-more-less-html__markup show-more-less-html__markup--clamp-after-5">
   <p><strong>We believe that great software is built by teams where collaboration, mutual respect and a drive for quality are front and centre. We want diverse perspectives, a passion for learning and we want people who care deeply about their work. We simply don't understand how long hours cultures are a source of pride or expected to produce excellence. We don't get how combative, political environments are meant to generate amazing teamwork. We don't want an environment where people dread going to work each day. If you feel the same way, please get in touch for a non-committal chat with a member of our team</strong></p>
   <p><br></p>
   <p><strong>We are Adaptive, where you’ll use the latest technology to design, build and operate bespoke, real-time, front-to-back solutions for tier-one investment banks and commodity trading firms financial clients using the latest technology, in flat teams where innovation and collaboration are the backbones of our success.</strong></p>
   <p><br></p>
   <p>As a Java Developer, you will</p>
   <ul>
    <li>participate in the team effort to build and release quality financial software in a timely manner.</li>
    <li>You will be involved in the technical design and implementation of a distributed, multi-region, multi-platform architecture.</li>
    <li>You will be working work in a test-driven, Agile development environment.</li>
   </ul>
   <p><br></p>
   <p><strong>Required skills and experience:</strong></p>
   <ul>
    <li>Solid, professional experience of server-side software development experience preferably in (but not restricted to) Java</li>
    <li>Knowledge of scripting language (e.g. Python)</li>
    <li>Passionate about building distributed, scalable, reliable, and performant software</li>
    <li>Experience with financial systems is a plus</li>
    <li>Deep knowledge of concurrency, resiliency, caching, HTTP and REST</li>
    <li>Even-tempered and able to remain focused on solving production issues when they arise</li>
    <li>Experience working in an Agile environment (Scrum, Kanban)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</li>
    <li>BSc/MSc in Computer Science or equivalent</li>
    <li>Excellent communication skills</li>
    <li>Good English language skills are great to have (but we do offer classes)</li>
    <li>Experience working with distributed teams</li>
   </ul>
   <p><br></p>
   <p><strong>Personal qualities:</strong></p>
   <ul>
    <li>Strong desire to raise the bar for your team technically</li>
    <li>Tenacious, curious, and collaborative in all aspects of your work</li>
    <li>A quick learner with excellent communication skills</li>
   </ul>
   <p><br></p>
   <p><strong>About us:</strong></p>
   <ul>
    <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Competitive Salary</li>
    <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Great benefits package</li>
    <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;No politics</li>
    <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;No cumbersome hierarchy: our teams feel free to speak up, to make suggestions and raise concerns</li>
    <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Collaborative team environment: we all work together, respect each other and pitch in</li>
    <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Smart, welcoming and motivated colleagues</li>
    <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Good work/life balance</li>
   </ul>
   <p><br></p>
   <p><strong>Some of our success stories include:</strong></p>
   <p><br></p>
   <p><em>An app store that allows users to browse available apps and install to their desktop without Administrator rights. The system provides an auto-update mechanism and also captures usage statistics</em></p>
   <p><br></p>
   <p><em>Adaptive brought our experience in large scale e-commerce platforms to quickly specify and&nbsp;agree&nbsp;an architecture with the client. The design enabled rapid development in the short term but also granted flexibility and agility in the long term.</em></p>
   <p><br></p>
   <p><strong>The Small Print</strong></p>
   <p>Please note that the successful candidate will need to have a background check.</p>
   <p>Adaptive's Privacy Notice for Candidates - https://weareadaptive.com/privacy-notice-applicants-adaptive-financial-consulting-ltd/</p>

 <div class="show-more-less-html__markup show-more-less-html__markup--clamp-after-5">
  <p><strong>We believe that great software is built by teams where collaboration, mutual respect and a drive for quality are front and centre. We want diverse perspectives, a passion for learning and we want people who care deeply about their work. We simply don't understand how long hours cultures are a source of pride or expected to produce excellence. We don't get how combative, political environments are meant to generate amazing teamwork. We don't want an environment where people dread going to work each day. If you feel the same way, please get in touch for a non-committal chat with a member of our team</strong></p>
  <p><br></p>
  <p><strong>We are Adaptive, where you’ll use the latest technology to design, build and operate bespoke, real-time, front-to-back solutions for tier-one investment banks and commodity trading firms financial clients using the latest technology, in flat teams where innovation and collaboration are the backbones of our success.</strong></p>
  <p><br></p>
  <p>As a Java Developer, you will</p>
  <ul>
   <li>participate in the team effort to build and release quality financial software in a timely manner.</li>
   <li>You will be involved in the technical design and implementation of a distributed, multi-region, multi-platform architecture.</li>
   <li>You will be working work in a test-driven, Agile development environment.</li>
  </ul>
  <p><br></p>
  <p><strong>Required skills and experience:</strong></p>
  <ul>
   <li>Solid, professional experience of server-side software development experience preferably in (but not restricted to) Java</li>
   <li>Knowledge of scripting language (e.g. Python)</li>
   <li>Passionate about building distributed, scalable, reliable, and performant software</li>
   <li>Experience with financial systems is a plus</li>
   <li>Deep knowledge of concurrency, resiliency, caching, HTTP and REST</li>
   <li>Even-tempered and able to remain focused on solving production issues when they arise</li>
   <li>Experience working in an Agile environment (Scrum, Kanban)&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</li>
   <li>BSc/MSc in Computer Science or equivalent</li>
   <li>Excellent communication skills</li>
   <li>Good English language skills are great to have (but we do offer classes)</li>
   <li>Experience working with distributed teams</li>
  </ul>
  <p><br></p>
  <p><strong>Personal qualities:</strong></p>
  <ul>
   <li>Strong desire to raise the bar for your team technically</li>
   <li>Tenacious, curious, and collaborative in all aspects of your work</li>
   <li>A quick learner with excellent communication skills</li>
  </ul>
  <p><br></p>
  <p><strong>About us:</strong></p>
  <ul>
   <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Competitive Salary</li>
   <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Great benefits package</li>
   <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;No politics</li>
   <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;No cumbersome hierarchy: our teams feel free to speak up, to make suggestions and raise concerns</li>
   <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;Collaborative team environment: we all work together, respect each other and pitch in</li>
   <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Smart, welcoming and motivated colleagues</li>
   <li>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;Good work/life balance</li>
  </ul>
  <p><br></p>
  <p><strong>Some of our success stories include:</strong></p>
  <p><br></p>
  <p><em>An app store that allows users to browse available apps and install to their desktop without Administrator rights. The system provides an auto-update mechanism and also captures usage statistics</em></p>
  <p><br></p>
  <p><em>Adaptive brought our experience in large scale e-commerce platforms to quickly specify and&nbsp;agree&nbsp;an architecture with the client. The design enabled rapid development in the short term but also granted flexibility and agility in the long term.</em></p>
